  \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \n  Threats that could lead to death (and other forms of high-severity violence) targeting people or places where threat is defined as any of the following:\n\n      \n              Statements of intent to commit high-severity violence; or \n        Calls for high-severity violence including content where no target is specified but a symbol represents the target and\/or includes a visual of an armament to represent violence; or \n        Statements advocating for high-severity violence; or \n        Aspirational or conditional statements to commit high-severity violence \n     \n      \n      Content that asks or offers services for hire to kill others (for example, hitmen, mercenaries, assassins) or advocates for the use of a hitman, mercenary or assassin against a target. \n     \n      Admissions, statements of intent or advocacy, calls to action, or aspirational or conditional statements to kidnap a target. \n     \n   Threats that lead to serious injury (mid-severity violence) towards private individuals, unnamed specified persons, minor public figures, high risk persons, or high risk groups where threat is defined as any of the following:\n\n      \n Statements of intent to commit violence; or \n        Statements advocating violence; or \n        Calls for mid-severity violence including content where no target is specified but a symbol represents the target; or \n        Aspirational or conditional statements to commit violence; or  \n   Content about other target(s) apart from private individuals, minor public figures, high risk persons, or high risk groups and any credible:\n      \n     \n          Statements of intent to commit violence; or \n          Calls for action of violence; or \n          Statements advocating for violence; or \n       Aspirational or conditional statements to commit violence \n   \n    \n\n      Threats that lead to physical harm (or other forms of lower-severity violence) towards private individuals (self-reporting required) or minor public figures where threat is defined as any of the following:\n         \n      \n            Private individuals (name and\/or face match are required) or minor public figures that includes:\n          \n       \n                Statements of intent, calls for action, advocating, aspirational or conditional statements to commit low-severity violence  \n              \n      \n    \n     Imagery of private individuals or minor public figures that has been manipulated to include threats of violence either in text or pictorial (adding bulls eye, dart, gun to head, etc.) \n        Content that exposes the identity or locations affiliated with any individual who is alleged to be a member of a designated and recognizable at-risk group, share familial and\/or romantic relationships with a member of an at-risk group or have performed professional activities in support of an at-risk group (except for political figures).\n \n        Instructions on how to make or use weapons if there\u2019s evidence of a goal to seriously injure or kill people, through:\n     \n          \n            Language explicitly stating that goal, or \n            Photos or videos that show or simulate the end result (serious injury or death) as part of the instruction \n            Unless the aforementioned content is shared as part of recreational self defense, for military training purposes, commercial video games, or news coverage (posted by Page or with news logo) \n          \n      \n     \n      Providing instructions on how to make or use explosives:\n         \n          \n            Unless there is clear context that the content is for a non-violent purpose (for example part of commercial video games, clear scientific\/educational purpose, fireworks, or specifically for fishing) \n          \n      \n   Any content containing statements of intent, calls for action, conditional or aspirational statements, or advocating for violence due to voting, voter registration, or the administration of outcome of an election \n\n      Statements of intent or advocacy, calls to action, or aspirational or conditional statements to bring weapons  to locations, including but not limited to places of worship, educational facilities polling places, or locations used to count votes or administer an election ( or encouraging others to do the same). \n     \n\n \n  \n  \n \n       For the following Community Standards, we require additional information and\/or context to enforce:  \n\n\n     \n       Do not post: \n  \n    Content that puts LGBTQI+ people at risk by revealing their sexual identity against their will or without permission \n Content that puts unveiled women at risk by revealing their images without veil against their will or without permission \n    Violent threats against law enforcement officers \n    Violent threats against people accused of a crime. We remove this content when we have reason to believe that the content is intended to cause physical harm \n    Misinformation and unverifiable rumors that contribute to the risk of imminent violence or physical harm \n Coded statements where the method of violence or harm is not clearly articulated, but the threat is veiled or implicit\n \n    Threats against election officials \n    Implicit statements of intent or advocacy, calls to action, or aspirational or conditional statements to bring armaments to locations, including but not limited to places of worship, educational facilities, polling places, or locations used to count votes or administer an election (or encouraging others to do the same). We may also restrict calls to bring armaments to certain locations where there are temporary signals of a heightened risk of violence or offline harm.  \n      \n      \n      \n      \n       \n\n     \n  \n\n     \n         \n    \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   We aim to prevent potential offline harm that may be related to content on Facebook. While we understand that people commonly express disdain or disagreement by threatening or calling for violence in non-serious ways, we remove language that incites or facilitates serious violence. We remove content, disable accounts, and work with law enforcement when we believe there is a genuine risk of physical harm or direct threats to public safety. We also try to consider the language and context in order to distinguish casual statements from content that constitutes a credible threat to public or personal safety. In determining whether a threat is credible, we may also consider additional information like a person's public visibility and the risks to their physical safety. \n  \n     In some cases, we see aspirational or conditional threats directed at terrorists and other violent actors (e.g. Terrorists deserve to be killed), and we deem those non credible absent specific evidence to the contrary.  \n  \n "},"dangerous_individuals_organizations":{"other_content":"\n   \n  \n    We do not allow the following people (living or deceased) or groups to maintain a presence (for example, have an account, Page, Group) on our platform: \n    \nTerrorist organizations and terrorists, which include:\n   \n \n\t Any non-state actor that:\n  \t \n       Engages in, advocates, or lends substantial support to purposive and planned acts of violence, \n       Which causes or attempts to cause death, injury or serious harm to civilians, or any other person not taking direct part in the hostilities in a situation of armed conflict, and\/or significant damage to property linked to death, serious injury or serious harm to civilians \n    \t With the intent to coerce, intimidate and\/or influence a civilian population, government, or international organization \n       In order to achieve a political, religious, or ideological aim. \n     \n   \n \n \n     \n \nHate organizations and their leaders and prominent members     \n \n   A hate organization is defined as:\n  \t \n    \t Any association of three or more people that is organized under a name, sign, or symbol and that has an ideology, statements, or physical actions that attack individuals based on characteristics, including race, religious affiliation, nationality, ethnicity, gender, sex, sexual orientation, serious \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   To encourage safety and compliance with common legal restrictions, we prohibit attempts by individuals, manufacturers, and retailers to purchase, sell, or trade non-medical drugs, pharmaceutical drugs, and marijuana. We also prohibit the purchase, sale, gifting, exchange, and transfer of firearms, including firearm parts or ammunition, between private individuals on Facebook. Some of these items are not regulated everywhere; however, because of the borderless nature of our community, we try to enforce our policies as consistently as possible. Firearm stores and online retailers may promote items available for sale off of our services as long as those retailers comply with all applicable laws and regulations. We allow discussions about sales of firearms and firearm parts in stores or by online retailers and advocating for changes to firearm regulation. Self-injury is defined as the intentional and direct injuring of the body, including self-mutilation and eating disorders. We want Facebook to be a space where people can share their experiences, raise awareness about these issues, and seek support from one another, which is why we allow people to discuss suicide and self-injury.\n    \n We work with organizations around the world to provide assistance to people in distress. We also talk to experts in suicide and self-injury to help inform our policies and enforcement. For example, we have been advised by experts that we should not remove live videos of self-injury while there is an opportunity for loved ones and authorities to provide help or resources. \n\n In contrast, we remove any content that identifies and negatively targets victims or survivors of self-injury or suicide seriously, humorously, or rhetorically. \n\n     Learn more about our suicide and self-injury policies and the resources that we provide.  \n     \n "},"child_nudity_sexual_exploitation":{"other_content":"\n   \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \nContent that depicts participation in or We do not tolerate this kind of behavior because it prevents people from feeling safe and respected on Facebook.  \n\n We distinguish between public figures and private individuals because we want to allow discussion, which often includes critical commentary of people who are featured in the news or who have a large public audience. For public figures, we remove attacks that are severe as well as certain attacks where the public figure is directly tagged in the post or comment. For private individuals, our protection goes further: we remove content that's meant to degrade or shame, including, for example, claims about someone's sexual activity. We recognize that bullying and harassment can have more of an emotional impact on minors, which is why our policies provide heightened protection for users between the ages of 13 and 18. \n\n Context and intent matter, and we allow people to share and re-share posts if it is clear that something was shared in order to condemn or draw attention to bullying and harassment. In certain instances, we require self-reporting because it helps us understand that the person targeted feels bullied or harassed. In addition to reporting such behavior and content, we encourage people to use  tools available on Facebook  to help protect against it. \n    \n     We also have a  Bullying Prevention Hub , which is a resource for teens, parents, and educators seeking support for issues related to bullying and other conflicts. It offers step-by-step guidance, including information on how to start important conversations about bullying. Learn more about what we\u2019re doing to protect people from bullying and harassment  here . \n   \n "},"human_exploitation":{"other_content":"\n   \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \n      Content or exhibit behavior that may lead to human exploitation, which includes any of the following:\n\n      \n        Sex Trafficking, covering minors and adults \n        The sale of children for illegal adoption\n         \n        Orphanage Trafficking and Orphanage Volun-tourism\n           \n        Forced Marriages\n         \n        Labor Exploitation (incl. bonded labor)\n         \n        Domestic Servitude\n         \n        Non-regenerative Organ Trafficking \n        Forced Criminal Activity (e.g. forced begging, forced drug trafficking) \n        Recruitment of Child Soldiers \n           \n\n      Content geared towards the:\n      \n        Recruitment of potential victims through force, fraud, coercion, enticement, deception, blackmail or other non-consensual acts. \n        Facilitation of human exploitation by coordinating, transporting, transferring, harboring or brokering of victims prior or during the exploitation.  \n        Exploitation of humans by promoting, depicting, or advocating for it. \n        \n      Content that offers or assists in smuggling of humans \n      \n         \n    \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   After consulting with outside experts from around the world, we are consolidating several existing exploitation policies that were previously housed in different sections of the Community Standards into one dedicated section that focuses on human exploitation and captures a broad range of harmful activities that may manifest on our platform. Experts think and talk about these issues under one umbrella \u2014 human exploitation.   \n     \n     \n     \n      In an effort to disrupt and prevent harm, we remove content that facilitates or coordinates the exploitation of humans, including human trafficking. We define human trafficking as the business of depriving someone of liberty for profit. It is the exploitation of humans in order to force them to engage   in commercial sex, labor, or other activities against their will. It relies on deception, force and coercion, and degrades humans by depriving them of their freedom while economically or materially benefiting others.   \n     \n     \n     \n      Human trafficking is multi-faceted and global; it can affect anyone regardless of age, socioeconomic background, ethnicity, gender, or location. It takes many forms, and any given trafficking situation can involve various stages of development. By the coercive nature of this abuse, victims cannot consent. \n     \n     \n     \n      While we need to be careful not to conflate human trafficking and smuggling, the two can be related and exhibit overlap. The United Nations defines human smuggling as the procurement or facilitation of illegal entry into a state across international borders. Without necessity for coercion or force, it may still result in the exploitation of vulnerable individuals who are trying to leave their country of origin, often in pursuit of a better life. Human smuggling is a crime against a state, relying on movement, and human trafficking is a crime against a person, relying on exploitation. \n \n cases may promote real-world violence. \n\n     We define hate speech as a direct attack on people based on what we call protected characteristics \u2014 race, ethnicity, national origin, religious affiliation, sexual orientation, caste, sex, gender, gender identity, and serious disease or disability. We protect against attacks on the basis of age when age is paired with another protected characteristic, and also provide certain protections for immigration status. We define attack as violent or dehumanizing speech,harmful stereotypes, statements of inferiority, or calls for exclusion or segregation. We separate attacks into three tiers of severity, as described below. \n\n     Sometimes people share content containing someone else\u2019s hate speech for the purpose of raising awareness or educating others. In some cases, words or terms that might otherwise violate our standards are used self-referentially or in an empowering way. People sometimes express contempt in the context of a romantic break-up. Other times, they use gender-exclusive language to control membership in a health or positive support group, such as a breastfeeding group for women only. In all of these cases, we allow the content but expect people to clearly indicate their intent, which helps us better understand why they shared it. Where the intention is unclear, we may remove the content. \n\n     In addition, we believe that people are more responsible when they share this kind of commentary using their authentic identity. \n\n     Click here to read our Hard Questions Blog  and learn more about our approach to hate speech. \n \n "},"graphic_violence":{"other_content":"\n   \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \n      Imagery of People   \n Videos of people or dead bodies in non-medical settings if they depict\n   \n  \t Dismemberment \n     Visible internal organs; partially decomposed bodies \n     Charred or burning people unless in the context of cremation or self-immolation when that action is a form of political speech or newsworthy \n     Victims of cannibalism \n     Throat-slitting \n        \n \n      Live streams of capital punishment of a person \n\n     \n    \n  \n   \n      \n  For the following content, we include a warning screen so that people are aware the content may be disturbing. We do this to avoid facilitating transactions that may involve trafficking, coercion, and non-consensual sexual acts. We also restrict sexually explicit language that may lead to solicitation because some audiences within our global community may be sensitive to this type of content and it may impede the ability for people to connect with their friends and the broader community.  \n "},"cruel_insensitive":{"other_content":"\n   \n  \n    Do not post: \n    \n      Content that depicts real people and laughs at or makes fun of their serious physical injury, starvation, or serious or fatal disease or disability.  \n   \n        Content that contains sadistic remarks and any visual or written depiction of real people experiencing premature death, serious physical injury, physical violence or  domestic violence. \n\n Imagery that depicts real animals that are visibly experiencing and being laughed at, made fun of, or contain sadistic remarks for any of the following (except staged animal vs. animal fights or animal fights in the wild):\n \n   premature death \n   serious physical injury (including mutilation) \n   physical violence from a human \n   \n      \n   \n ","policy_rationale":"\n   We believe that people share and connect more freely when they do not feel targeted based on their vulnerabilities. We are a service for more than two billion people to freely express themselves across countries and cultures and in dozens of languages. \n     We recognize how important it is for Facebook to be a place where people feel empowered to communicate, and we take seriously our role in keeping abuse off our service. That\u2019s why we\u2019ve  developed a set of Community Standards  that outline what is and is not allowed on Facebook. Our policies are based on feedback from our community and the advice of experts in fields such as technology, public safety and human rights. To ensure that everyone\u2019s voice is valued, we take great care to craft policies that are inclusive of different views and beliefs, in particular those of people and communities that might otherwise be overlooked or marginalized. \n   \n         \n     REITERATING OUR COMMITMENT TO VOICE \n     The goal of our Community Standards has always been to  create a place for expression and give people a voice . This has not and will not change. Building community and bringing the world closer together depends on people\u2019s ability to share diverse views, experiences, ideas and information. We want people to be able to talk openly about the issues that matter to them, even if some may disagree or find them objectionable. In some cases, we allow content for public awareness which would otherwise go against our Community Standards \u2013 if it is newsworthy and in the public interest. We do this only after weighing the public interest value against the risk of harm and we look to international human rights standards to make these judgments. As such, we consider the newsworthiness of content posted by anyone, including news organizations and individuals users. For example, we have allowed content that graphically depicts war or the consequences of war where it is important to public discourse.  \n    \n     Our commitment to expression is paramount, but we recognize the internet creates new and increased opportunities for abuse. For these reasons, when we limit expression, we do it in service of one or more of the following values: \n   \n       \n\n     Authenticity:  We want to make sure the content people are seeing on Facebook is authentic. We believe that authenticity creates a better environment for sharing, and that\u2019s why we don\u2019t want people using Facebook to misrepresent who they are or what they\u2019re doing.\n \n    \n    \n      \n    \n     Safety:  We are committed to making Facebook a safe place. Expression that threatens people has the potential to intimidate, exclude or silence others and isn\u2019t allowed on Facebook. \n  \n    \n  \n    \n    \n     Privacy:  We are committed to protecting personal privacy and information. Privacy gives people the freedom to be themselves, and to choose how and when to share on Facebook and to connect more easily.\n \n        \n  \n    \n     Dignity:  We believe that all people are equal in dignity and rights. We expect that people will respect the dignity of others and not harass or degrade others. \n    \n\n\n    \n    \n     Our Community Standards apply to everyone, all around the world, and to all types of content. They\u2019re designed to be comprehensive \u2013 for example, content that might not be considered hateful may still be removed for violating a different policy. We recognize that words mean different things or affect people differently depending on their local community, language, or background. We work hard to account for these nuances while also applying our policies consistently and fairly to people and their expression. Our enforcement of these standards relies on information available to us. In some cases, this means that we may not detect content and behavior that violates these standards, and in others,  enforcement may be limited to circumstances where we have been provided with additional information and context. \n\n     People can report potentially violating content, including Pages, Groups, Profiles, individual content, and comments. We also give people control over their own experience by allowing them to\n       block ,   unfollow \n       or \n        hide  people and posts.\n       \n\n     The consequences for violating our Community Standards vary depending on the severity of the violation and the person's history on the platform. For instance, we may warn someone for a first violation, but if they continue to violate our policies, we may restrict their ability to post on Facebook or disable their profile. We also may notify law enforcement when we believe there is a genuine risk of physical harm or a direct threat to public safety. \n     Our Community Standards are a guide for what is and isn\u2019t allowed on Facebook. It is in this spirit that we ask members of the Facebook community to follow these guidelines. \n     \nPlease note that the US English version of the Community Standards reflects the most up-to-date set of the policies and should be used as the master document. \n   \n "},"dummyElem":{"__m":"__elem_fc9f538f_0_0"},"acrossTransitions":false,"clobberSiblings":false,"preloader":null,"bigPipeContext":{"__bigPipeContext":1},"lid":"6900192964056571418-0","nonBlockingPreloaders":null,"moduleID":"CommunityStandardsRoot.react","tracePolicy":null}]],["Animation"],["VideosRenderingInstrumentation","storeRenderTime",["__elem_a648e52c_0_0"],[{"__m":"__elem_a648e52c_0_0"}]],["__inst_a648e52c_0_0"],["VideoDisplayTimePlayButton","register",["__elem_8937e029_0_0","__elem_0bcc40a7_0_0"],[{"__m":"__elem_8937e029_0_0"},{"__m":"__elem_0bcc40a7_0_0"}]],["__inst_3f1e98e4_0_0"],["__inst_0bcc40a7_0_0"],["__inst_ebb64f7c_0_0"],["__inst_98d9a45e_0_0"],["__inst_21a8c1d4_0_0"],["__inst_dbb8a0b1_0_0"],["__inst_74f26af1_0_0"],["__inst_6d29ee41_0_0"],["__inst_70dbca80_0_0"],["VideoDashPrefetchCache","loadVideo",[],[{"videoID":1415167278571737,"manifest":[],"video":[{"url":"https:\/\/video-lax3-2.xx.fbcdn.net\/v\/t42.1790-2\/18824400_1415174128571052_5055827053203423232_n.mp4?_nc_cat=106&ccb=2&_nc_sid=5aebc0&efg=eyJ2ZW5jb2RlX3RhZyI6ImRhc2hfdjNfMTI4MF9jcmZfMjNfaGlnaF8zLjFfZnJhZ18yX3ZpZGVvIn0\u00253D&_nc_ohc=wzkpN8veVHUAX_fZCCq&_nc_ht=video-lax3-2.xx&oh=7c63d249e034e0d67e4876a0595cf7e2&oe=5FC29216","start":0,"end":956,"segment_type":"init","mime_codec":"video\/mp4; class="_12bc _11wv"><div><div class="_297a"><div class="_21c0"><div class="_21c1">INTRODUCTION</div><div class="_4n96"><p class="_3i--">Chaque jour, les personnes utilisent Facebook pour partager des expriences, communiquer avec leurs proches et crer des communauts. Notre service permet  plus de deuxmilliards de personnes de sexprimer librement, au-del des frontires et des cultures, dans des dizaines de langues.</p><p class="_3i--">Nous sommes conscients de limportance pour Facebook doffrir un espace incitant les gens  communiquer, et nous prenons trs au srieux notre rle afin dcarter les abus de notre service. Cest la raison pour laquelle nous avons <a href="https://lm.facebook.com/l.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fnewsroom.fb.com%2Fnews%2F2019%2F04%2Finsidefeed-community-standards-development-process%2F&amp;h=AT3TsKOpSZvMcirzICjS6OrNuwkliwRHWzpweHTIFGu97niqbSOk5li2Px-eEGZRNrFZZMSOck46c6sSwkQ9OBfk1gwCG1_DiAJu1KRSZKM7xKncTgXZKu4KvcIwJRjw6abDvFbmuHGPxfrmV-HT" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" data-lynx-mode="asynclazy">cr un ensemble de Standards de la communaut</a> qui expliquent ce qui est autoris, ou non, sur Facebook. Nos politiques sont fondes sur les retours de notre communaut et lavis de spcialistes dans des domaines comme les technologies, la scurit publique et les droits de lhomme. Pour nous assurer que tout le monde est respect, nous nous efforons de crer des politiques qui prennent en compte les diffrents points de vue et croyances, surtout ceux des personnes et communauts marginalises ou ngliges.</p><div style="text-align: center"><i class="img _257 _4cef img _2sxw" style="background-image: url(&#039;https\3a //scontent-cdt1-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.2365-6/30179729_1969747913355382_7724706176021037056_n.png?_nc_cat\3d 1\26 ccb\3d 2\26 _nc_sid\3d ad8a9d\26 _nc_ohc\3d qSQTbHl6sd8AX_6zDbo\26 _nc_ht\3d scontent-cdt1-1.xx\26 oh\3d 0c28ff708edb316f14ebb3808c6dad30\26 oe\3d 5FEAA8FA&#039;);background-repeat:no-repeat;background-size:100% 100%;-webkit-background-size:100% 100%;width:166px;height:163px;"></i></div><br /><div class="_21c1">RITRER NOTRE ENGAGEMENT POUR LEXPRESSION</div><p class="_3i--">Lobjectif de nos Standards de la communaut a toujours t de <a href="https://lm.facebook.com/l.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fnewsroom.fb.com%2Fnews%2F2018%2F08%2Fhard-questions-free-expression%2F&amp;h=AT0szNFtyWJPY3CGZ-m_IMbsyK5nA84sravq9Ig4WkB7wnVmSRsm7Mp9x-dIaGVnAxXiC-5P7BqvsZ0TQa6a_kwc6Xs1kWJazj36yqerNUe3H3D1cC5C3hTS_dZl6Gg18TNMHLCIpZw-_GIFJAlt" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" data-lynx-mode="asynclazy">crer un espace dexpression et de donner une voix aux personnes</a>. Cela na pas chang et cela ne changera pas. Pour crer des communauts et rapprocher les gens, il faut pouvoir partager des points de vue, des expriences, des ides et des informations varis. Nous souhaitons que les personnes puissent sexprimer ouvertement sur les sujets qui comptent pour elles, mme si dautres peuvent marquer leur dsaccord ou y trouveraient  redire. Dans certains cas, nous autorisons -  des fins de sensibilisation - la publication de contenu qui va  lencontre de nos Standards de la communaut sil est pertinent et dintrt public. Nous ne prenons cette dcision quaprs avoir valu limpact positif pour lintrt public par rapport  la nuisance potentielle, et nous nous appuyons sur les principes universels des droits de lHomme. Nous prenons ainsi en considration lintrt mdiatique du contenu publi par tout individu, y compris les agences de presse et les utilisateurs particuliers. Par exemple, nous avons autoris des contenus illustrant graphiquement la guerre ou les consquences de la guerre lorsquils savrent importants pour la rflexion publique.</p><p class="_3i--">Notre engagement en faveur de la libert dexpression est primordial, mais nous sommes conscients quInternet est une source de formes dabus nouvelles et croissantes. Lorsque nous limitons la libert dexpression, nous le faisons pour le respect de lune ou de plusieurs des valeurs suivantes:</p><br /><div style="text-align: center"><i class="img _257 _4cef img _2sxw" style="background-image: url(&#039;https\3a //scontent-cdt1-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.2365-6/70546071_460725341450782_7389006442629431296_n.png?_nc_cat\3d 1\26 ccb\3d 2\26 _nc_sid\3d ad8a9d\26 _nc_ohc\3d xhqbBc8M97kAX84quXW\26 _nc_ht\3d scontent-cdt1-1.xx\26 oh\3d 44e969aec1f9bf8db2684c64c76cc040\26 oe\3d 5FE7C0A5&#039;);background-repeat:no-repeat;background-size:100% 100%;-webkit-background-size:100% 100%;width:172px;height:162px;"></i></div><p class="_3i--"><b>Authenticit:</b> Nous voulons nous assurer que le contenu que les personnes voient sur Facebook est authentique. Nous sommes convaincus que lauthenticit cre un meilleur environnement pour le partage, et nous ne voulons donc pas que les personnes qui utilisent Facebook mentent sur leur identit ou leurs activits. </p><div style="text-align: center"><i class="img _257 _4cef img _2sxw" style="background-image: url(&#039;https\3a //scontent-cdt1-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.2365-6/30179798_233411330550983_830803110640222208_n.png?_nc_cat\3d 1\26 ccb\3d 2\26 _nc_sid\3d ad8a9d\26 _nc_ohc\3d sNaUMXNR_t4AX-h-Mxn\26 _nc_ht\3d scontent-cdt1-1.xx\26 oh\3d b896371831883272b91c5d2d00471950\26 oe\3d 5FEADC63&#039;);background-repeat:no-repeat;background-size:100% 100%;-webkit-background-size:100% 100%;width:166px;height:163px;"></i></div><p class="_3i--"><b>Scurit:</b> Nous nous engageons  faire de Facebook un endroit sr. Les formes dexpression qui menacent les autres peuvent les intimider, les exclure ou les rduire au silence, et ne sont pas autorises sur Facebook.</p><br /><div style="text-align: center"><i class="img _257 _4cef img _2sxw" style="background-image: url(&#039;https\3a //scontent-cdt1-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.2365-6/70744027_1120870694776290_6189555203662938112_n.png?_nc_cat\3d 1\26 ccb\3d 2\26 _nc_sid\3d ad8a9d\26 _nc_ohc\3d MqRcJu9Sbi8AX9ZQ4QU\26 _nc_ht\3d scontent-cdt1-1.xx\26 oh\3d 001ac20325ada20beb0e23c8fafc9e89\26 oe\3d 5FE7C750&#039;);background-repeat:no-repeat;background-size:100% 100%;-webkit-background-size:100% 100%;width:172px;height:162px;"></i></div><p class="_3i--"><b>Confidentialit:</b> Nous nous engageons  protger votre vie prive et vos informations. La confidentialit donne aux personnes la libert dtre elles-mmes, et de choisir quand et comment elles partagent des informations sur Facebook. Cela facilite la cration de liens. </p><div style="text-align: center"><i class="img _257 _4cef img _2sxw" style="background-image: url(&#039;https\3a //scontent-cdt1-1.xx.fbcdn.net/v/t39.2365-6/70707979_539090683561979_6815354865225564160_n.png?_nc_cat\3d 1\26 ccb\3d 2\26 _nc_sid\3d ad8a9d\26 _nc_ohc\3d JqY0jPrrK1kAX9Dk3Of\26 _nc_ht\3d scontent-cdt1-1.xx\26 oh\3d fe64c8884c1185b6bfba76e96ec4b41a\26 oe\3d 5FE934C2&#039;);background-repeat:no-repeat;background-size:100% 100%;-webkit-background-size:100% 100%;width:159px;height:167px;"></i></div><p class="_3i--"><b>Dignit:</b> Nous pensons que chacun mrite les mmes droits et la mme dignit. Nous attendons de chaque personne quelle respecte la dignit dautrui, et quelle ne harcle pas et ne rabaisse pas les autres.</p><p class="_3i--">Nos Standards de la communaut sappliquent  tout le monde, partout dans le monde, et  tous les types de contenu. Ils ont t conus pour tre exhaustifs. Par exemple, du contenu qui ne serait pas considr comme haineux pourrait malgr tout tre supprim parce quil enfreint une autre politique. Nous savons que les mots ont diffrentes significations et naffectent pas les personnes de la mme manire selon leur communaut locale, leur langue et leurs origines. Nous mettons tout en uvre pour prendre en compte ces nuances tout en appliquant nos politiques de manire juste et cohrente pour chaque utilisateur et sa libert dexpression. Notre application de ces standards repose sur les informations dont nous disposons. Dans certains cas, cela signifie quil se peut que nous ne dtections pas les contenus et les comportements qui volent ces standards, et dans d&#039;autres, [l&#039;application peut tre limite aux circonstances dans lesquelles nous avons reu ce contexte et ces informations supplmentaires].</p><p class="_3i--">Il est possible de signaler du contenu potentiellement en infraction, notamment les Pages, les Groupes, les Profils, le contenu individuel ou des commentaires. Nous les aidons aussi  contrler leur propre exprience en leur permettant de <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/168009843260943?ref=ccs">bloquer</a>, de <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/276458109035418?ref=ccs"> se dsabonner</a> ou <a href="https://www.facebook.com/help/268028706671439?ref=ccs"> de masquer</a> des personnes et des publications. </p><p class="_3i--">La violation de nos Standards de la communaut engendre diverses consquences qui varient en fonction de la gravit de linfraction et des antcdents de la personne sur la plate-forme. Nous pouvons, par exemple, avertir une personne dune premire infraction, mais si celle-ci persiste  enfreindre notre rglement, nous pouvons limiter sa capacit  publier du contenu sur Facebook ou dsactiver son profil.
